STAT

variable font

axis ordering

MS NID 6

Postscript names should not be longer then 29 characters. May cause issues in PDF.

Is longer:
'neithergreaterthannorequivalentto
neitherlessthannorequivalentto'

Pass

Noto Sans Mono Regular (NotoSansMono[wdth,wght].ttf)
